<gmapID>0x80dd260f89c4b06d:0xb81d40d1a12ea1d1<//gmapID>< review>
This was my first time at LensCrafters and I am very glad I decided on this location. Everyone was incredibly helpful, kind, and easy to speak with.

I met with Miguel at the front desk to get checked in and fill out my paperwork. Miguel was incredibly friendly and helpful from beginning to end, and took the time to explain the different forms I was completing. After, I was greeted by Liz to go through the routine consultation (pictures of eye, air puff eye test, etc.) and I felt comfortable the entire time. She was so friendly and communicated every part of each process to me. For my eye exam, I met with Elaine and started my eye exam. She was very helpful and explained my options with great detail. Once I got my prescription, Mai helped me practice putting on and taking out my contacts, with getting my frames, and payment which was quick and easy as well. I was originally scared to try contacts because of the application process, but Mai helped me taught me some helpful tips and I was able to put in and remove my contacts very easily. I was fitted for contacts, received new frames, and got new sunglasses all in under 2 hours!

Everyone was very easy to speak to and were great to work with. I highly recommend coming to the Westminster Mall location and I will definitely be returning in the future! Thank you so much!<//review>

I am writing this review to let everyone know that LensCrafters at Westminster mall is amazing!
The store is really cool with SO many designer and affordable frames, you won‚Äôt believe it.
I wear progressive lenses and they can be very challenging to fit for me so that I can see properly.
With progressive lenses millimeters are like miles, and they must be fitted to your frame and face ACCURATELY. If your pupillary distance is measured but is off by even a small amount, you will NOT be able to see out of all of the the fields of vision correctly.
THIS LensCrafters at Westminster Mall located at 2056 Westminster Ca 92683 did an unbelievable job. They fit my progressive lenses to me with such expertise, and I cannot even truly express how well I can see through these new lenses! < review>
I wanted to have just a routine eye exam because I want to purchase a Ray-Ban prescription sunglasses. I was being pressured to have a DFE Dilation exam. I asked about any side effects and I was told that my eyes would be sensitive to light and will not be able to see clearly. I was told by a technician named Terry that the Intermediate exam w/o DFE does not cause any side effects and it will replace the DFE Dilation. After I had the  Intermediate exam, I was told by the eye doctor ( Dr. Chang, O.D.) that what Terry told me is not true! Dr. Chang told myself that I need to have the DFE Dilation and when I refused due to the side effects, I was told by Dr. Chang to sign the Informed Refusal form. I don't understand why I am being told one thing and then another! These people are using scare tactics to make me pay more for the eye exam. I was also told by Dr. Chang that I need to have the Progressive Lens. I later found out that at certain distances, it causes blurred vision due to the technology not being perfected yet unlike Bifocals lenses. I should have just purchased the Single-Vision lenses instead of Progressive Lenses.</review>

<rating>1< /rating>< Review>
Overall management of the apartment complex was very disappointing.

- Roaches were present throughout 2 years of living in the apartment - we did request insect spray about 6 times. It's understandable that it's very hard to eradicate roaches from an apartment complex, but at least acknowledge that there is a problem and attempt to do something about it.
-  Loud noises - in the past 6 months the area around apartment 556 became absolutely unbearable to sleep. We have complained multiple times to the staff that it's very noisy after 10 pm. Plus skateboarders would be present throughout the entire weekend making a lot of noise.
- Inflexible management that didn't make the move out experience easy at all. We didn't notify the office one month ahead about our move out intentions (this is totally on us), though we did manage to move out 2 weeks earlier than we otherwise should have been. The management did apply prorated amount anyways. We were also told that it would be possible for us to get these money back if someone moves in before the official date we needed to move out by. Funny thing, I got a call from the office asking how my move out experience was 3 days after everything was already moved. It didn't seem like the team is interested in trying to have someone move in.
- Absolutely insane parking situation. Coming back home on Sunday evening means: good luck with finding any free spots at all. The newly implemented program did make the situation slightly better, though it didn't look like it actually fixed anything at all.

Overall, I have to say that I'm very disappointed by Las Palmas. I have had quite a few friends living in apartment complexes owned by Irvine Company, and no one has any similar problems.<//Review>

<Name>Tom Sly< /Name>< Review>
Beautiful interior & Atmosphere - unfortunately it all stopped there!

We were in town for the Ragnar relay race. After running 200 miles over 32 hours, we were looking for a nice glass of wine and a hearty meal.
The manager was quite accommodating in provide a booth, which looked more comfortable to our aching bodies.
From that point after, this restaurant was a complete disappointment.

The waiter described one of their bottles of cabernet completely wrong.  It was nothing like he described. Fortunately, we tried a glass of it first.  We ordered another bottle after he checked with the  bartender for a bottle that was less fruit forward and a bit more oakey.

He served the Cab in chardonnay glasses . Hard to believe that any restaurant in wine country would do this.  But we were told they had a big lunch crowd and didn't have enough clean cab glasses. We saw a few at the bar and asked if he would mind getting them for us.  He found three, then later a fourth.

The delicata squash soup was thin with no body or flavor.  It was served with a teaspoon not a soup spoon.  We sent both bowls back.  The baby field  green salad with estero gold reserve cheese was described by the waiter as similar to a goat cheese salad with a red wine vinaigrette.  The cheese was actually a shaved Italian cheese. Not even close.  How can a nice restaurant have a waiter that doesn't know the difference between a hard Italian cheese and goat cheese?

Chicken and wedge salad was slightly better but still diner quality, not what you'd expect from a restaurant that has invested as much as Brannan's has in their beautiful hard wood walls and ceilings, rich leather booths, inviting classic bar, stone fireplace with the elk mount above etc.    The pork chops were a prime quality bone in chop, but was equally as lackluster in it's preparation.   The   spaetzle was overcooked and mushy, the sweet garlic sauce was lacking any real flavor.   Mac & cheese side dish was just ok.  Hard to believe that a fine restaurant cannot make a rich cheesy, casserole of macaroni and cheese.   And I think that says enough.  Brannans looks like a fine restaurant but doesn't deliver.

I can understand that a restaurant might hire a completely uninformed local as a waiter during a busy weekend and it's clear that is what we got.   He could not describe a single dish other than read off the menu.   However, when everything that comes out of the kitchen is equally as disappointing, it really makes you wonder how this place can even keep it's doors open.

For those of us that don't live in wine country and come here expecting impressive wining and dining...Brannans is definitely not the place.< /Review>

<rate>5</rate>< review>
I ordered the tofu and vegetables to go. While I waited I watched the kitchen through a large glass window. It gave the space a slightly upscale vibe unexpected for a Chinese place in Chico. Watching the staff work the wok and food gave me nostalgia for my time in Guanzhou, watching street vendors expertly cook noodle dishes in front of me. The avacado green walls gave the room a warm and inviting ambiance. The food I watched coming out was all vibrant looking and delicious smelling. Vegetables were brightly colored (so they were fresh) and dumplings were plump and steaming. The staff was attentive and friendly and asked everyone how their day was going. I'm so glad I decided to pop in. The dish I ordered was excellent, tasty and spicy and crunchy. This is going to be my new favorite Chico Chinese place.<//review>

< text>
This place is really great! If you are looking for a corporate-style bowling experience, this is NOT the place. They have 8 Lanes, so lanes are limited, but the waiting list moves quickly. The staff was extremely helpful and struck a great balance between professional and casual. I saw lockers for rent and an advertisement for a leauge. They have a good selection of arcade games, and the snack bar has a dining area. The food is extremely generous and tasty; you may consider breaking your diet for their burgers. I also saw 6 taps; mostly Firestone brews, but they also had SLO Brew as well. I saw some unused taps, so their selection may regularly change. Prices are extremely affordable. This is a fantastic place for a great time and is a must-stop when visiting Pismo.<//text>

<Date>1508182675030</Date>< username>
Paul Malarik Jr</username>
< review>
This is a great place for visiting relatives & their kids.  There are games, junk food, and best of all a clean modern bowling alley.  For some reason, the lanes are not too crowded & you can usually snag one.

The balls are just OK, but the shoes are too slippery IMHO.  The scoring is computerized, so you do not have to mess with the old pens/ paper system.

I also like their air hockey game.

As far as I know, this is the only bowling alley within dozens, if not hundreds of miles...so this is it.

For those who are as out of shape as I am, you will hurt the next few days if you swing the ball like you did 40 odd years ago!<//review>
